<script>
    (function(window, document){
        var key = "featured-sliderIndex";
        var storageAvailable = function(type){
            //https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/Web_Storage_API/Using_the_Web_Storage_API
            try {
                var storage = window[type],
                        x = '__storage_test__';
                storage.setItem(x, x);
                storage.removeItem(x);
                return true;
            }
            catch(e) {
                return false;
            }
        };


        var slider = document.querySelectorAll('.rotating-image-slider');

        if (slider.length > 0){
            var indexs = [];
            if (storageAvailable('localStorage')) {
                if (localStorage[key]!=undefined){
                    indexs = localStorage[key].split(',');
                }
            }
            for (var i=0; i<slider.length; i++){
                var el = slider[i];

                var images= el.querySelectorAll(".image-wrapper");
                if ( images.length > 0 ){
                    var index = (indexs[i]==undefined||indexs[i]==""||indexs[i]==null)?0:parseInt(indexs[i])+1;
                    if (images.length <= index || isNaN(index)) {
                        index = 0;
                    }
                    indexs[i] = index;
                    images[index].className += "active";

                
                images[index].className += " shown";
                document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function(event) {
                    analytics.trackEcommercePromoImpression(
                        images[index].querySelectorAll("a")[0].getAttribute('href'),
                        'featured_Slider',
                        'featured_Slider_'+images[index].querySelectorAll("a")[0].getAttribute('data-position')
                    );
                });
                
                }

                // Add className only if having at least two images (show nav buttons).
                if (images.length > 1) {
                    var navBtn = el.querySelectorAll(".nav-btn");
                    navBtn[index].className += "active";
                }

            }
            if (storageAvailable('localStorage')) {
                localStorage[key] = indexs;
            }
        }

    })(window, document);
</script>

        <script>
        
        function registerColorbox() {
            colorboxDesktop.showIFrame("/register", {
                "innerWidth": 430,
                "innerHeight": 290
            });
        }

        
        window.addEventListener("message", receiveMessage, false);
        function receiveMessage(event) {
            if (event.origin.indexOf(window.location.host) == -1)
                return;
            if ( typeof event.data == "string")
            {
                if (event.data.indexOf('resize') != -1) {
                    var elements = event.data.split(':');
                    colorboxDesktop.resize({height: elements[1]});
                }
                else{
                    switch(event.data){
                        case 'reload_email':
                        case 'reload_facebook':
                            var sPageURL = parent.location.search.substring(1);
                            var sURLVariables = sPageURL.split('&');
                            var reloadFlag = true;
                            var newSearch = '';
                            var platform = event.data.split('_')[1];
                            for (var i = 0; i < sURLVariables.length; i++) {
                                if (i > 0)
                                    newSearch += '&';

                                var sParameterName = sURLVariables[i].split('=');
                                if (sParameterName[0] == 'register' && sParameterName[1] == 'true') {
                                    sParameterName[1] = 'false';
                                    reloadFlag = false;
                                }
                                newSearch += sParameterName[0] + '=' + sParameterName[1];
                            }
                            if (typeof analytics != 'undefined' && analytics != null){
                                analytics.trackRegisterSuccess('','','');
                            }

                            setTimeout(function(){// wait for analytics above
                                if (reloadFlag) {
                                    location.reload(true);
                                }
                                else {
                                    location.replace(location.protocol + '//' + location.host + location.pathname + '?' + newSearch);
                                }
                            }, 300);

                            break;
                        case 'loadLoginPage':
                            location.replace(location.protocol + '//' + location.host + "/login");
                            break;
                        case 'loadForgotPasswordPage':
                            location.replace(location.protocol + '//' + location.host + "/login/pw/request");
                            break;
                        case 'loginSuccess':
                            location.replace(location.protocol + '//' + location.host + location.pathname + '?register=false');
                            break;
                        case 'snsLinkUpdated':
                            location.replace(location.protocol + '//' + location.host + "/my-account?snsRedirect=linkAutoFailure");
                            break;
                    }
                }
            }
            else if (typeof event.data === "object") {
                typeof event.data["actionName"] === "string" && Logger && Logger.log("[receiveMessage] Received message: ", event.data);

                switch (event.data["actionName"]) {
                    case "checkoutRegister":
                        location.replace(event.data["redirectUrl"]);
                        break;
                    case "loginSuccess":
                        location.replace(event.data["redirectUrl"]);
                        break;
                    case "reload":
                        location.replace(location.protocol + '//' + location.host + location.pathname + '?' + location.search.replace("register=true", "register=false"));
                        break;
                    case "snsLinkUpdated":
                        location.replace(location.protocol + '//' + location.host + "/my-account?snsRedirect=linkAutoFailure");
                        break;
                    case "colorboxResize":
                        colorboxDesktop.resize({
                            "innerWidth": parseInt(event.data["innerWidth"]),
                            "innerHeight": parseInt(event.data["innerHeight"])
                        });
                        break;
                }
            }
        }
        
        
        if(hktvCommon.priorIEVerLimit(9)){
            $('body').addClass('ie_fallback');
        }

        <script>
	hktvCommon.addStringResources({
		"beTheFirstToBuy": "成為首位買家",
		"soldOut": "售罄",

</script><script>
    (function($, window, document){

        (function(f) {
            window.setSliderTimeout = f(window.setTimeout);   // extends the global function!
            window.setSliderInterval = f(window.setInterval); // extends the global function!
        })(function(f) {
            return function(c, t) {
                var a = [].slice.call(arguments, 2);    // gathers the extra args
                return f(function() {
                    c.apply(this, a);                   // passes them to your function
                }, t);
            };
        });

        
        var slider = $(".rotating-image-slider");
        var navBtnGlobal = $(".nav-btn", slider);
        var nextBtn = $(".button.next", slider);
        var prevBtn = $(".button.prev", slider);
        var timeoutIDs = [];
        var indexs = [];
        var key = "featured-sliderIndex";

        function slideInit(i) {
            if (i!=undefined){
                timeoutIDs[i] = window.setSliderTimeout(animateSlide, 5000, i);
            }else{
                if (hktvCommon.storageAvailable('localStorage')) {
                    if (localStorage[key]!=undefined){
                        indexs = localStorage[key].split(',');
                    }
                }
                slider.each(function(j){
                    // define which banner should be active is done by inline js
                    // we set the timer only in here
                    timeoutIDs.push(window.setSliderTimeout(animateSlide, 5000, j));
                });
            }
        }
        function animateSlide(j) {
            var images=$(".image-wrapper", slider[j]);
            if (images.length>1){
                images.each(function(index){
                    if ($(this).hasClass("active")){
                        $(this).removeClass("active");
                        var navBtn = $(".nav-btn", slider[j])
                        navBtn.eq(index).removeClass("active");
                        var nextIndex = (images.length>index+1)?index+1:0;
                        images.eq(nextIndex).addClass("active");

                        
                        if($(window).scrollTop() < (images.offset().top + images.height()) && !images.eq(nextIndex).hasClass("shown")){
                            images.eq(nextIndex).addClass("shown");
                            // TODO : trigger impression
                            analytics.trackEcommercePromoImpression(
                                images.eq(nextIndex).find('a').attr('href'),
                                'featured_Slider',
                                'featured_Slider_'+images.eq(nextIndex).find('a').data('position')
                            );
                        }
                        

                        navBtn.eq(nextIndex).addClass("active");
                        timeoutIDs[j]=(window.setSliderTimeout(animateSlide, 5000, j));

                        //update index
                        indexs[j] = nextIndex ;
                        if (hktvCommon.storageAvailable('localStorage')) {
                            localStorage[key] = indexs;
                        }


                        return false;
                    }
                });


            }

        }
        function clearAnimateSlide(i) {
            if (i!=undefined){
                window.clearTimeout(timeoutIDs[i]);
            }else{
                for (var id in timeoutIDs){
                    window.clearTimeout(timeoutIDs[id]);
                }
                timeoutIDs = [];
                indexs = [] ;
                if (hktvCommon.storageAvailable('localStorage')) {
                    localStorage.removeItem(key);
                }

            }
        }

        nextBtn.click(function(){
            var self = this;
            slider.each(function(i){
                if ($.contains(this, self)){
                    var images=$(".image-wrapper", this);
                    var navBtn = $(".nav-btn", this);
                    images.removeClass("active");
                    navBtn.removeClass("active");

                    //update index
                    var index;
                    if(indexs[i] >= navBtn.length-1){
                        index = 0 ;
                    }
                    else{
                        index = ++indexs[i];
                    }
                    indexs[i] = index ;

                    if (hktvCommon.storageAvailable('localStorage')) {
                        localStorage[key] = indexs;
                    }

                    images.eq(index).addClass("active");

                    
                    if(!images.eq(index).hasClass("shown")){
                        images.eq(index).addClass("shown");
                        analytics.trackEcommercePromoImpression(
                            images.eq(index).find('a').attr('href'),
                            'featured_Slider',
                            'featured_Slider_'+images.eq(index).find('a').data('position')
                        );
                    }
                    

                    navBtn.eq(index).addClass("active");
                    clearAnimateSlide(i);
                    slideInit(i);
                }
            });
        });
        prevBtn.click(function(){
            var self = this;
            slider.each(function(i){
                if ($.contains(this, self)){
                    var images=$(".image-wrapper", this);
                    var navBtn = $(".nav-btn", this);
                    images.removeClass("active");
                    navBtn.removeClass("active");

                    //update index
                    var index;
                    if(indexs[i] == 0){
                        index = navBtn.length-1;
                    }
                    else{
                        index = --indexs[i];
                    }
                    indexs[i] = index;

                    if (hktvCommon.storageAvailable('localStorage')) {
                        localStorage[key] = indexs;
                    }

                    images.eq(index).addClass("active");

                    
                    if(!images.eq(index).hasClass("shown")){
                        images.eq(index).addClass("shown");
                        analytics.trackEcommercePromoImpression(
                            images.eq(index).find('a').attr('href'),
                            'featured_Slider',
                            'featured_Slider_'+images.eq(index).find('a').data('position')
                        );
                    }
                    

                    navBtn.eq(index).addClass("active");
                    clearAnimateSlide(i);
                    slideInit(i);
                }
            });
        });
        navBtnGlobal.on("click", function(){
            var index = $(this).data("index");
            var self = this;
            slider.each(function(i){
                if ($.contains(this, self)){
                    var images=$(".image-wrapper", this);
                    var navBtn = $(".nav-btn", this);
                    images.removeClass("active");
                    navBtn.removeClass("active");

                    //update index
                    indexs[i] = index ;
                    if (hktvCommon.storageAvailable('localStorage')) {
                        localStorage[key] = indexs;
                    }

                    images.eq(index).addClass("active");

                    
                    if(!images.eq(index).hasClass("shown")){
                        images.eq(index).addClass("shown");
                        analytics.trackEcommercePromoImpression(
                            images.eq(index).find('a').attr('href'),
                            'featured_Slider',
                            'featured_Slider_'+images.eq(index).find('a').data('position')
                        );
                    }
                    

                    navBtn.eq(index).addClass("active");
                    clearAnimateSlide(i);
                    slideInit(i);
                }
            });
        });
        slideInit();
    })(jQuery, window, document);


</script>
<script>
        var onPageChange = function(pageState){
            var page = hktvCommon.queryStringExtracter(location.href).page;
            if (page > 1) {
                $('#product-container').removeClass('col4').addClass('col3right');
                $('.rotating-image-slider').hide();
                $('#featured-product-container').hide();
            }

    <script>
    
    $(".rotating-image-slider").on('click', 'a', function() {
        
        analytics.trackEcommercePromoClick(
                $(this).attr('href'),
                'featured'+'_Slider',
                'featured'+'_Slider_'+$(this).data('position')
        );
        
    });

    
    $('#nav-bar').on('click', '.tab-dropdown a', function() {
        analytics.trackEvent('featured', 'Editor_Picks', 'Tab');
    });

    
    $('#cat-tree').on('click', 'a', function() {
        analytics.trackEvent('featured', $(this).attr('href'), 'Body');
    });

    
    $("#featured-product-container").on('click', 'a.product-brief', function() {
        var analytics_zone = 'featured';
        analytics.trackEvent(analytics_zone, analytics_zone + '_PDP_Main', $(this).data('code'));
    });
    $("#product-container").on('click', 'a.product-brief', function() {
        var analytics_zone = 'featured';
        var pos = $(this).index() + 1;
        var page = hktvCommon.queryStringExtracter(location.search).page;
        if (typeof page == 'undefined')
            page = 1;
        analytics.trackEvent(analytics_zone, analytics_zone + '_PDP_' + page + '_' + pos, $(this).data('code'));
    });

    
    $("#pagination-container").on('click', 'a.arrow-left.enable', function() {
        var analytics_zone = 'featured';
        analytics.trackEvent(analytics_zone, analytics_zone + '_Prev', 'N/A');
    });
    $("#pagination-container").on('click', 'a.arrow-right.enable', function() {
        var analytics_zone = 'featured';
        analytics.trackEvent(analytics_zone, analytics_zone + '_Next', 'N/A');
    });
</script><input type="hidden" value="page-landing" class="landingCurrentPage">

</body>

</html>
